Loading your savegame caused OpenTTD to crash.
This is most likely caused by a missing NewGRF or a NewGRF that
has been loaded as replacement for a missing NewGRF. OpenTTD
cannot easily determine whether a replacement NewGRF is of a newer
or older version.
It will load a NewGRF with the same GRF ID as the missing NewGRF.
This means that if the author makes incompatible NewGRFs with the
same GRF ID, OpenTTD cannot magically do the right thing. In most
cases, OpenTTD will load the savegame and not crash, but this is an
exception.
Please load the savegame with the appropriate NewGRFs installed.
The missing/compatible NewGRFs are:
NewGRF %08X (checksum %s) not found.
  Loaded NewGRF "%s" (checksum %s) with same GRF ID instead.
NewGRF %08X (%s) not found; checksum %s.
This is probably caused by a corruption in the savegame.
Please file a bug report and attach this savegame.

Restarts a game. It tries to reproduce the exact same map as the game started with.
 * restarting games started in another version might create another map due to difference in map generation.
 * restarting games based on scenarios, loaded games or heightmaps will start a new game based on the settings stored in the scenario/savegame.
 * if you started from a savegame / scenario / heightmap, that exact same savegame / scenario / heightmap will be loaded.
